43 /**
44   * typical profile / account json exchange format, we could add picture and some other nice stuff?
45   *
46   * @param email
47   * @param accountSubject
48   * @param firstname
49   * @param lastname
50   */
51 case class ProfileJs(email: EmailAddress,
52                      accountSubject: String,
53                      firstname: String,
54                      lastname: String)
55 
56 /**
57   * here password is compulsory
58   *
59   * @param email
60   * @param accountSubject
61   * @param firstname
62   * @param lastname
63   * @param password
64   */
65 case class RegisterJs(email: EmailAddress,
66                       accountSubject: String,
67                       firstname: String,
68                       lastname: String,
69                       password: String)
70 
71 /**
72   *
73   * @param config
74   * @param cacheApi
75   * @param emailService
76   * @param collectionsService
77   * @param sessionHolder
78   * @param passwordHashing
79   */
80 @Singleton
81 class UserController @Inject()(config: Configuration,
82                                cacheApi: CacheApi,
83                                emailService: EmailService,
84                                collectionsService: OwcCollectionsService,
85                                sessionHolder: SessionHolder,
86                                override val passwordHashing: PasswordHashing) extends Controller with ClassnameLogger with Security {
87 
88   lazy private val appTimeZone: String = configuration.getString("datetime.timezone").getOrElse("Pacific/Auckland")
89   lazy private val googleClientSecret: String = configuration.getString("google.client.secret")
90     .getOrElse("client_secret.json")
91   val cache: play.api.cache.CacheApi = cacheApi
92   val configuration: play.api.Configuration = config
93   val gauthRedirectUrl = "postmessage"
94 
95   /**
96     * self registering for user accounts
97     * will create "preliminary" user account and send out confirmation email with unique link to "activate" account
98     * we could require app dunctions only to be used by "ACTIVE" users wit hconfirmed email
99     *
100     * @return
101     */
102   def registerUser: Action[JsValue] = Action(parse.json) { request =>
103 
104     request.body.validate[RegisterJs].fold(
105       errors => {
106         logger.error(JsError.toJson(errors).toString())
107         val error = ErrorResult("Error while validating request.", Some(JsError.toJson(errors).toString))
108         BadRequest(Json.toJson(error)).as(JSON)
109       },
110       jsuser => {
111         // found none, good ...
112         sessionHolder.viaTransaction { implicit connection =>
113           UserDAO.findUserByEmailAddress(jsuser.email).fold {
114             // found none, good, create user
115             val regLinkId = java.util.UUID.randomUUID().toString()
116             val cryptPass = passwordHashing.createHash(jsuser.password)
117 
118             val newUser = User(jsuser.email,
119               s"local:${jsuser.email}",
120               jsuser.firstname,
121               jsuser.lastname,
122               cryptPass,
123               s"${StatusToken.REGISTERED}:$regLinkId",
124               ZonedDateTime.now.withZoneSameInstant(ZoneId.of(appTimeZone)))
125 
126             UserDAO.createUser(newUser).fold {
127               logger.error("User create error.")
128               val error = ErrorResult("User create error.", None)
129               BadRequest(Json.toJson(error)).as(JSON)
130             } { user =>
131               val emailWentOut = emailService.sendRegistrationEmail(jsuser.email, "Please confirm your GW HUB account", jsuser.firstname, regLinkId)
132               logger.info(s"New user registered. Email went out $emailWentOut")
133               // creating default collection only after registration, account is only barely usable here
134               Ok(Json.toJson(user.asProfileJs()))
135             }
136           } { user =>
137             // found user with that email already
138             logger.error("Email already in use.")
139             val error = ErrorResult("Email already in use.", None)
140             BadRequest(Json.toJson(error)).as(JSON)
141           }
142         }
143       })
144   }
145 
146   /**
147     * confirm the registration link, based on that email is confirmed,
148     * could add more require logic to app functions that want an established email account
149     *
150     * @param linkId
151     * @return
152     */
153   def registerConfirm(linkId: String): Action[AnyContent] = Action { request =>
154     // check db laststatustoken, get user etc, update status
155     val uuidTest = Try(java.util.UUID.fromString(linkId))
156     uuidTest match {
157       case Success(v) => {
158         // logger.debug("Result of " + uuidTest.get.toString + " is: " + v)
159         sessionHolder.viaTransaction { implicit connection =>
160           UserDAO.findRegisteredUsersWithRegLink(linkId).headOption.fold {
161             // found none, if more than one take head of the list
162             logger.error("Unknown registration link.")
163             // flash error message
164             // BadRequest(Json.obj("status" -> "ERR", "message" -> "Unknown registration link."))
165             Redirect("/#/register")
166           } { user =>
167             // good, update regstatus and send confirmation email
168             val updateUser = User(
169               user.email,
170               user.accountSubject,
171               user.firstname,
172               user.lastname,
173               "***",
174               s"${StatusToken.ACTIVE}:REGCONFIRMED",
175               ZonedDateTime.now.withZoneSameInstant(ZoneId.of(appTimeZone)))
176 
177             UserDAO.updateNoPass(updateUser).fold {
178               logger.error("User update error.")
179               // Redirect("/#/register")
180               // flash error message?
181               val error = ErrorResult("Error while updating user registration", None)
182               InternalServerError(Json.toJson(error)).as(JSON)
183             } { user =>
184               val emailWentOut = emailService.sendConfirmationEmail(user.email, "Your GW HUB account is now active", user.firstname)
185               // all good here, creating default collection (Unit)
186               val userOwcDoc = collectionsService.createUserDefaultCollection(user)
187               // maybe should also do the full login thing here? how does that relate with the alternative Google Oauth thing
188               userOwcDoc.fold {
189                 logger.error("Couldn't create user default collection.")
190                 val error = ErrorResult("Error while creatin user default collection.", None)
191                 InternalServerError(Json.toJson(error)).as(JSON)
192               } { owcDoc =>
193                 logger.info(s"Registered user ${user.accountSubject} confirmed email ${user.email}. " +
194                   s"Email went out $emailWentOut. User Collection ${owcDoc.id.toString}")
195                 Redirect("/#/login")
196               }
197             }
198           }
199         }
200       }
201       case Failure(e) => {
202         // wrong uuid format even
203         logger.error("Info from the exception: " + e.getMessage)
204         // maybe flash error message
205         Redirect("/#/register")
206       }
207     }
208   }

210   /**
211     * get own profile based on security token
212     *
213     * @return
214     */
215   def userSelf: Action[Unit] = HasToken(parse.empty) {
216     token =>
217       cachedSecUserEmail =>
218         implicit request =>
219           sessionHolder.viaConnection(implicit connection =>
220             UserDAO.findUserByEmailAsString(cachedSecUserEmail).fold {
221               logger.error("User email not found.")
222               val error = ErrorResult("User email not found.", None)
223               BadRequest(Json.toJson(error)).as(JSON)
224             } { user =>
225               Ok(Json.toJson(user.asProfileJs()))
226             }
227           )
228   }
229 
230   /**
231     * get own profile based on security token
232     *
233     * @return
234     */
235   def deleteSelf: Action[Unit] = HasToken(parse.empty) {
236     token =>
237       cachedSecUserEmail =>
238         implicit request =>
239           sessionHolder.viaTransaction { implicit connection =>
240             UserDAO.findUserByEmailAsString(cachedSecUserEmail).fold {
241               logger.error("User email not found.")
242               val error = ErrorResult("User email not found.", None)
243               BadRequest(Json.toJson(error)).as(JSON)
244             } { user =>
245               val result = UserDAO.deleteUser(user)
246               if (result) {
247                 cache.remove(token)
248                 Ok.discardingCookies(DiscardingCookie(name = AuthTokenCookieKey))
249               } else {
250                 logger.error(s"User ${user.accountSubject} could not be deleted.")
251                 val error = ErrorResult("Sorry, we could not delete your account.", None)
252                 BadRequest(Json.toJson(error)).as(JSON)
253               }
254             }
255           }
256   }
257 
258   /**
259     * get user's profle, currently only one's own profile (token match)
260     *
261     * @param email
262     * @return
263     */
264   def getProfile(email: String): Action[Unit] = HasToken(parse.empty) {
265     token =>
266       cachedSecUserEmail =>
267         implicit request =>
268           sessionHolder.viaConnection(implicit connection =>
269             UserDAO.findUserByEmailAsString(email).fold {
270               logger.error("User email not found.")
271               val error = ErrorResult("User email not found.", None)
272               BadRequest(Json.toJson(error)).as(JSON)
273             } { user =>
274               // too much checking here?
275               if (user.email.value.equals(email) && cachedSecUserEmail.equals(email)) {
276                 Ok(Json.toJson(user.asProfileJs()))
277               } else {
278                 logger.error("User email Security Token mismatch.")
279                 val error = ErrorResult("User email Security Token mismatch.", None)
280                 Forbidden(Json.toJson(error)).as(JSON)
281               }
282             }
283           )
284   }
285 
286   /**
287     * update user's profile, can "never" touch password, password update is separate
288     *
289     * @return
290     */
291   def updateProfile: Action[JsValue] = HasToken(parse.json) {
292     token =>
293       cachedSecUserEmail =>
294         implicit request =>
295 
296           val profileResult = request.body.validate[ProfileJs]
297           profileResult.fold(
298             errors => {
299               val error = ErrorResult("Could not validate request.", Some(JsError.toJson(errors).toString()))
300               BadRequest(Json.toJson(error)).as(JSON)
301             },
302             incomingProfileJs => {
303               sessionHolder.viaTransaction { implicit connection =>
304                 // looking first for the HasToken auth subject
305                 UserDAO.findUserByEmailAsString(cachedSecUserEmail).fold {
306                   logger.error("User Security Token mismatch.")
307                   val error = ErrorResult("User Security Token mismatch.", None)
308                   Forbidden(Json.toJson(error)).as(JSON)
309                 } { hasTokenDbUser =>
310                   // This should be you. we don't change the accountSubject. email change is ok but needs to be extra validated
311                   if (hasTokenDbUser.email.equals(incomingProfileJs.email)) {
312                     // email didn't change, good, let's update your profile in the database (but not password nor accountsubject)
313                     val updateUser = hasTokenDbUser.copy(email = incomingProfileJs.email,
314                       firstname = incomingProfileJs.firstname,
315                       lastname = incomingProfileJs.lastname,
316                       laststatustoken = s"${StatusToken.ACTIVE}:PROFILEUPDATE",
317                       laststatuschange = ZonedDateTime.now.withZoneSameInstant(ZoneId.of(appTimeZone)))
318 
319                     UserDAO.updateNoPass(updateUser).fold {
320                       logger.error("Could not update User.")
321                       val error = ErrorResult("Could not update user.", None)
322                       BadRequest(Json.toJson(error)).as(JSON)
323                     } { user =>
324                       val emailWentOut = emailService.sendProfileUpdateInfoEmail(user.email, "Your account profile information was updated", user.firstname)
325                       logger.info(s"User profile updated. Email went out $emailWentOut")
326                       Ok(Json.toJson(user.asProfileJs()))
327                     }
328                   } else {
329                     // check if new email is used already by another user than yourself
330                     UserDAO.findUserByEmailAddress(incomingProfileJs.email).fold {
331 
332                       // found none, good, let's update your profile in the database (but not password nor accountsubject)
333                       val regLinkId = java.util.UUID.randomUUID().toString()
334                       val updateUser = hasTokenDbUser.copy(email = incomingProfileJs.email,
335                         firstname = incomingProfileJs.firstname,
336                         lastname = incomingProfileJs.lastname,
337                         laststatustoken = s"${StatusToken.EMAILVALIDATION}:$regLinkId",
338                         laststatuschange = ZonedDateTime.now.withZoneSameInstant(ZoneId.of(appTimeZone)))
339 
340                       UserDAO.updateNoPass(updateUser).fold {
341                         logger.error("Could not update User.")
342                         val error = ErrorResult("Could not update user.", None)
343                         BadRequest(Json.toJson(error)).as(JSON)
344                       } { user =>
345                         val emailWentOut = emailService.sendNewEmailValidationEmail(user.email, "Please confirm your new email address", user.firstname, regLinkId)
346                         logger.info(s"User profile updated with email change. Email went out $emailWentOut with reglink: $regLinkId")
347                         Ok(Json.toJson(user.asProfileJs()))
348                       }
349                     } { dbuser =>
350                       // found one, that means the email is already in use, ABORT
351                       logger.error("Email already in use.")
352                       val error = ErrorResult("Email already in use.", None)
353                       BadRequest(Json.toJson(error)).as(JSON)
354                     }
355                   }
356                 }
357               }
358             })
359 
360   }
361 
362   /**
363     * should require "double check" in gui to issue this, requires to accept and store new session secret
364     *
365     * @return
366     */
367   def updatePassword(): Action[JsValue] = HasToken(parse.json) {
368     token =>
369       cachedSecUserEmail =>
370         implicit request =>
371           request.body.validate[PasswordUpdateCredentials].fold(
372             errors => {
373               logger.error(JsError.toJson(errors).toString())
374               val error = ErrorResult("Could not validate request.", Some(JsError.toJson(errors).toString()))
375               BadRequest(Json.toJson(error)).as(JSON)
376             },
377             valid = credentials => {
378               // find user in db
379               sessionHolder.viaTransaction { implicit connection =>
380                 UserDAO.findUserByEmailAddress(credentials.email).fold {
381                   logger.error("User not found.")
382                   val error = ErrorResult("User not found", None)
383                   BadRequest(Json.toJson(error)).as(JSON)
384                 } { dbuser =>
385                   // compare password
386                   if (passwordHashing.validatePassword(credentials.oldPassword, dbuser.password)) {
387                     val newCryptPass = passwordHashing.createHash(credentials.newPassword)
388                     val updateUser = dbuser.copy(
389                       password = newCryptPass,
390                       laststatustoken = s"${StatusToken.ACTIVE}:PASSWORDUPDATE",
391                       laststatuschange = ZonedDateTime.now.withZoneSameInstant(ZoneId.of(appTimeZone)))
392 
393                     UserDAO.updatePassword(updateUser).fold {
394                       logger.error("Password update error.")
395                       val error = ErrorResult("Password update error.", None)
396                       BadRequest(Json.toJson(error)).as(JSON)
397                     } { user =>
398                       val uaIdentifier: String = request.headers.get(UserAgentHeader).getOrElse(UserAgentHeaderDefault)
399                       cache.remove(token)
400                       emailService.sendPasswordUpdateEmail(user.email, "Password Update on GW HUB", user.firstname)
401                       val newtoken = passwordHashing.createSessionCookie(user.email, uaIdentifier)
402                       cache.set(newtoken, user.email.value)
403                       Ok(Json.obj("status" -> "OK", "token" -> newtoken, "email" -> user.email.value))
404                         .withCookies(Cookie(AuthTokenCookieKey, newtoken, None, httpOnly = false))
405                     }
406                   } else {
407                     logger.error("Password update error, not matching.")
408                     val error = ErrorResult("Password update error, not matching.", None)
409                     BadRequest(Json.toJson(error)).as(JSON)
410                   }
411                 }
412               }
413             })
414   }
415 
416   /**
417     *
418     * @return
419     */
420   def resetPasswordRequest: Action[JsValue] = Action(parse.json) { request =>
421     request.body.validate[LoginCredentials].fold(
422       errors => {
423         logger.error(JsError.toJson(errors).toString())
424         val error = ErrorResult("Could not validate request.", Some(JsError.toJson(errors).toString()))
425         BadRequest(Json.toJson(error)).as(JSON)
426       },
427       valid = credentials => {
428         // find user in db
429         sessionHolder.viaTransaction { implicit connection =>
430           UserDAO.findUserByEmailAddress(credentials.email).fold {
431             logger.error("User email not found.")
432             val error = ErrorResult("User email not found.", None)
433             BadRequest(Json.toJson(error)).as(JSON)
434           } { user =>
435             val resetLink = java.util.UUID.randomUUID().toString
436             // good, update regstatus and send confirmation email
437             val updateUser = user.copy(laststatustoken = s"${StatusToken.PASSWORDRESET}:$resetLink",
438               laststatuschange = ZonedDateTime.now.withZoneSameInstant(ZoneId.of(appTimeZone)))
439 
440             UserDAO.updateNoPass(updateUser).fold {
441               logger.error("User reset password request update error.")
442               // flash error message?
443               val error = ErrorResult("User reset password request update error.", None)
444               BadRequest(Json.toJson(error)).as(JSON)
445               // Redirect("/#/register")
446             } { user =>
447               emailService.sendResetPasswordRequestEmail(user.email, "Password Update on GW HUB", user.firstname, resetLink)
448               logger.info(s"Registered user ${user.email} requested reset password. Email went out")
449               Ok(Json.obj("status" -> "OK", "email" -> user.email.value, "message" -> "Email went out"))
450             }
451           }
452         }
453       })
454   }
455 
456   /**
457     *
458     * @param linkId
459     * @return
460     */
461   def resetPasswordRedeem(linkId: String): Action[JsValue] = Action(parse.json) { request =>
462     // check db laststatustoken, get user etc, update status
463     val uuidTest = Try(java.util.UUID.fromString(linkId))
464     uuidTest match {
465       case Success(v) => {
466         sessionHolder.viaTransaction { implicit connection =>
467           UserDAO.findUsersByPassResetLink(linkId).headOption.fold {
468             logger.error("Unknown password reset link.")
469             Redirect("/#/register")
470           } { user =>
471             // good, update password and status and send confirmation email
472             request.body.validate[LoginCredentials].fold(
473               errors => {
474                 logger.error(JsError.toJson(errors).toString())
475                 val error = ErrorResult("Could not validate request.", Some(JsError.toJson(errors).toString()))
476                 BadRequest(Json.toJson(error)).as(JSON)
477               },
478               valid = credentials => {
479                 val cryptPass = passwordHashing.createHash(credentials.password)
480                 val updateUser = User(
481                   user.email,
482                   user.accountSubject,
483                   user.firstname,
484                   user.lastname,
485                   cryptPass,
486                   s"${StatusToken.ACTIVE}:PASSWORDUPDATED",
487                   ZonedDateTime.now.withZoneSameInstant(ZoneId.of(appTimeZone)))
488 
489                 UserDAO.updatePassword(updateUser).fold {
490                   logger.error("User update error.")
491                   // flash error message?
492                   // BadRequest(Json.obj("status" -> "ERR", "message" -> "User update error."))
493                   Redirect("/#/login")
494                 } { user =>
495                   val emailWentOut = emailService.sendPasswordUpdateEmail(user.email, "Password Update on GW HUB", user.firstname)
496                   Redirect("/#/login")
497                 }
498               })
499 
500           }
501         }
502       }
503       case Failure(e) => {
504         // wrong uuid format even
505         logger.error("Info from the exception: " + e.getMessage)
506         // maybe flash error message
507         Redirect("/#/register")
508       }
509     }
510   }

513   /**
514     * part of OAuth2 Flow for Google Login in
515     *
516     * @return
517     */
518   def gconnect: Action[JsValue] = Action(parse.json) { implicit request =>
519     request.body.validate[GAuthCredentials].fold(
520       errors => {
521         logger.error(JsError.toJson(errors).toString())
522         val error = ErrorResult("Could not validate request.", Some(JsError.toJson(errors).toString()))
523         BadRequest(Json.toJson(error)).as(JSON)
524       },
525       valid = credentials => {
526         if (!new java.io.File(googleClientSecret).exists) {
527           val error = ErrorResult("Service JSON file not available", None)
528           InternalServerError(Json.toJson(error)).as(JSON)
529         } else {
530           // do lots of Google OAuth2 stuff
531           val clientSecrets = GoogleClientSecrets.load(
532             JacksonFactory.getDefaultInstance(), new FileReader(googleClientSecret))
533 
534           // 988846878323-bkja0j1tgep5ojthfr2e92ao8n7iksab.apps.googleusercontent.com
535           val clientId = clientSecrets.getDetails().getClientId()
536           logger.debug(s"clientId $clientId")
537           // Specify the same redirect URI that you use with your web
538           // app. If you don't have a web version of your app, you can
539           // specify an empty string.
540           val tokenResponse: GoogleTokenResponse = new GoogleAuthorizationCodeTokenRequest(
541             new NetHttpTransport(),
542             JacksonFactory.getDefaultInstance(),
543             "https://www.googleapis.com/oauth2/v4/token",
544             clientId,
545             clientSecrets.getDetails().getClientSecret(),
546             credentials.authcode,
547             gauthRedirectUrl).execute()
548 
549           val accessToken = tokenResponse.getAccessToken()
550           // Use access token to call API
551           val credential = new GoogleCredential().setAccessToken(accessToken)
552           // Get profile info from ID token
553           val idToken: GoogleIdToken = tokenResponse.parseIdToken()
554           val payload = idToken.getPayload()
555           // Use this value as a key to identify a user.
556           val userId = payload.getSubject()
557           val email = payload.getEmail()
558           val emailVerified = payload.getEmailVerified()
559           // get further payload things that is easy in java but needs to work in scala too
560           val name = Option(payload.get("name").asInstanceOf[String])
561           val pictureUrl = Option(payload.get("picture").asInstanceOf[String])
562           val locale = Option(payload.get("locale").asInstanceOf[String])
563           val familyName = Option(payload.get("family_name").asInstanceOf[String])
564           val givenName = Option(payload.get("given_name").asInstanceOf[String])
565           if ((credentials.accesstype.equalsIgnoreCase("LOGIN") || credentials.accesstype.equalsIgnoreCase("REGISTER")) &&
566             emailVerified && EmailAddress.isValid(email)) {
567 
568             val emailAddress = EmailAddress(email)
569             // viaConnection lookup email block
570             val firstUserLookup = sessionHolder.viaConnection { implicit connection =>
571               UserDAO.findUserByEmailAddress(emailAddress)
572             }
573 
574             firstUserLookup.fold {
575               // 'error, no user': well, must be a new user coming through from Google
576               val cryptPass = passwordHashing.createHash(UUID.randomUUID().toString)
577 
578               val newUser = User(emailAddress,
579                 s"google:${userId}",
580                 givenName.getOrElse(name.getOrElse(emailAddress.mailbox.value)),
581                 familyName.getOrElse(""),
582                 cryptPass,
583                 s"${StatusToken.ACTIVE}:REGCONFIRMED",
584                 ZonedDateTime.now.withZoneSameInstant(ZoneId.of(appTimeZone)))
585 
586               val createUserCall = sessionHolder.viaConnection { implicit connection =>
587                 UserDAO.createUser(newUser)
588               }
589 
590               createUserCall.fold {
591                 logger.error("User create error.")
592                 val error = ErrorResult("Error while creating user", None)
593                 InternalServerError(Json.toJson(error)).as(JSON)
594               } { createdUser =>
595                 val emailWentOut = emailService.sendConfirmationEmail(createdUser.email, "Your GW HUB account is now active", createdUser.firstname)
596                 // all good here, creating default collection (Unit)
597                 val userOwcDocTransaction = sessionHolder.viaTransaction { implicit connection =>
598                   collectionsService.createUserDefaultCollection(createdUser)
599                 }
600 
601                 userOwcDocTransaction.fold {
602                   logger.error(s"Couldn't create user default collection for ${createdUser.accountSubject}.")
603                   val error = ErrorResult("Error while creating user default collection.", None)
604                   InternalServerError(Json.toJson(error)).as(JSON)
605                 } { owcDoc =>
606                   logger.info(s"New user registered ${createdUser.accountSubject}. Email went out $emailWentOut. " +
607                     s"User Collection ${owcDoc.id.toString}")
608                   val uaIdentifier: String = request.headers.get(UserAgentHeader).getOrElse(UserAgentHeaderDefault)
609                   // logger.debug(s"Logging in email from $uaIdentifier")
610                   val token = passwordHashing.createSessionCookie(createdUser.email, uaIdentifier)
611                   cache.set(token, createdUser.email.value)
612                   Ok(Json.obj("status" -> "OK", "token" -> token, "email" -> createdUser.email.value, "userprofile" -> createdUser.asProfileJs()))
613                     .withCookies(Cookie(AuthTokenCookieKey, token, None, httpOnly = false))
614                 }
615               }
616             } { existingUser =>
617               val uaIdentifier: String = request.headers.get(UserAgentHeader).getOrElse(UserAgentHeaderDefault)
618               // logger.debug(s"Logging in email from $uaIdentifier")
619               val token = passwordHashing.createSessionCookie(existingUser.email.value, uaIdentifier)
620               cache.set(token, existingUser.email.value)
621               Ok(Json.obj("status" -> "OK", "token" -> token, "email" -> existingUser.email.value, "userprofile" -> existingUser.asProfileJs()))
622                 .withCookies(Cookie(AuthTokenCookieKey, token, None, httpOnly = false))
623             }
624 
625           } else {
626             logger.error("Invalid accesstype requested")
627             val error = ErrorResult("Invalid accestype requested", None)
628             BadRequest(Json.toJson(error)).as(JSON)
629           }
630         }
631       }
632     )
633   }
634 
635 
636   /**
637     * Disconnect the Google login
638     *
639     * @return
640     */
641   def gdisconnect: Action[Unit] = HasToken(parse.empty) {
642     token =>
643       email =>
644         implicit request =>
645           cache.remove(token)
646           // do some Google OAuth2 unregisteR
647           Ok.discardingCookies(DiscardingCookie(name = AuthTokenCookieKey))
648   }

651     *
652     * @return
653     */
654   def oauth2callback: Action[AnyContent] = Action {
655     Redirect("/#/account")
656   }
